<html><head></head><body><div style="--fade-in-animation: fade-in-new-response 150ms cubic-bezier(0.3,0,0.8,0.15); animation: auto ease 0s 1 normal none running none; padding-top: 30px; position: relative; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Mo's algorithm</span>&nbsp;is&nbsp;<mark style="border-radius: 4px; background-size: 200% 100%; padding: 0px 2px; animation: 0.75s cubic-bezier(0.05, 0.7, 0.1, 1) 0.25s 1 normal forwards running highlight-animation;">a powerful square root decomposition technique used to solve&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">offline range queries</span>&nbsp;on a static array</mark>. It reorders queries to minimize the work needed to move from one query range to the next, often achieving a time complexity of&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><span style="display: inline;"><div style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 110.789px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">The algorithm works by maintaining a "sliding window"&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><span style="display: inline;"><div style="position: relative; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.74em" height="0.653em" viewBox="0 -0.653 0.74 0.653" style="vertical-align: 0em; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">]</text></svg></div></span></span></span>&nbsp;and two pointers. Instead of recalculating the answer for every query from scratch, it moves the pointers from the previous query's range to the current one by adding or removing elements one by one.<span><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 241px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: var(--EPacR--tQAWtd,12px) var(--EPacR--fHZGNe,16px); font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; margin-block: var(--EPacR--Mhy5Ac,0) var(--EPacR--tlBMye,12px); padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Offline Queries</span>: All queries are known beforehand so they can be reordered.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; margin-block: var(--EPacR--Mhy5Ac,0) var(--EPacR--tlBMye,12px); padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Static Data</span>: The underlying array does not change (no updates).</span></li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; margin-block: var(--EPacR--Mhy5Ac,0) var(--EPacR--tlBMye,12px); padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Efficient Updates</span>: You can easily&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">add(x)</code>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">)</text></svg></div></span></span></span>&nbsp;time.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px; white-space: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 241px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 20px;"><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal; margin-block: 0px 12px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Decomposition</span>: Divide the array of size&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative;     </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">global</span><span> curr_sum
    curr_sum += arr[idx]

</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">def</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">remove</span><span>(</span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">idx</span><span>):
    </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">global</span><span> curr_sum
    curr_sum -= arr[idx]

</span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;"># Inside the query loop:</span><span>
</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">while</span><span> currL &gt; L: currL -= </span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">1</span><span>; add(currL)

font-size: 1px" transform="translate(1.0844,0)">𝑁</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.333em" height="0.853em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.333 0.853" style="vertical-align: -0.177em; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">1. The Strategy<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">We divide the array into&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">blocks</span>&nbsp;of size&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><msqrt><mi>𝑁</mi></msqrt></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="1.879em" height="1.331em" viewBox="0 -1.1155 1.879 1.331" style="vertical-align: -0.2155em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.928,0)">𝑁</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,-0.0435)">√</text><line x1="0.928" y1="-0.9835" x2="1.879" y2="-0.9835" stroke-width="0.066" stroke="#E6E8F0"></line></svg></div></span></span>.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ol style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 20px;"><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal; margin-block: 0px 12px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Primary Sort:</span>&nbsp;Group queries by the&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">block index</span>&nbsp;of their left pointer (<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝐿</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.708em" height="0.653em" viewBox="0 -0.653 0.708 0.653" style="vertical-align: 0em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝐿</text></svg></div></span></span>).</span></li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal; margin-block: 0px 12px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Secondary Sort:</span>&nbsp;Within the same block, sort by the right pointer (<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝑅</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.74em" height="0.653em" viewBox="0 -0.653 0.74 0.653" style="vertical-align: 0em; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></li></ol><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">2. Why This Works<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Think of the&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝐿</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.708em" height="0.653em" viewBox="0 -0.653 0.708 0.653" style="vertical-align: 0em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝐿</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝑅</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.74em" height="0.653em" viewBox="0 -0.653 0.74 0.653" style="vertical-align: 0em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑅</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;pointers like two people walking along the array:<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: var(--EPacR--tQAWtd,12px) var(--EPacR--fHZGNe,16px); font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; margin-block: var(--EPacR--Mhy5Ac,0) var(--EPacR--tlBMye,12px); padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">The&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝐿</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.708em" height="0.653em" viewBox="0 -0.653 0.708 0.653" style="vertical-align: 0em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝐿</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;pointer:</span>&nbsp;Since&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝐿</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.708em" height="0.653em" viewBox="0 -0.653 0.708 0.653" style="vertical-align: 0em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝐿</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;stays within the same block (size&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><msqrt><mi>𝑁</mi></msqrt></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="1.879em" height="1.331em" viewBox="0 -1.1155 1.879 1.331" style="vertical-align: -0.2155em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.928,0)">𝑁</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,-0.0435)">√</text><line x1="0.928" y1="-0.9835" x2="1.879" y2="-0.9835" stroke-width="0.066" stroke="#E6E8F0"></line></svg></div></span></span>) for many queries, it only wiggles a little bit (<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><span style="display: inline;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.732em" height="0.68em" viewBox="0 -0.669 0.732 0.68" style="vertical-align: -0.011em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑂</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.333em" height="0.853em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.333 0.853" style="vertical-align: -0.177em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">(</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="1.879em" height="1.331em" viewBox="0 -1.1155 1.879 1.331" style="vertical-align: -0.2155em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.928,0)">𝑁</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,-0.0435)">√</text><line x1="0.928" y1="-0.9835" x2="1.879" y2="-0.9835" stroke-width="0.066" stroke="#E6E8F0"></line></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.333em" height="0.853em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.333 0.853" style="vertical-align: -0.177em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">)</text></svg></div></span></span></span>&nbsp;movement) between each query. Across all&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝑄</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.781em" height="0.819em" viewBox="0 -0.667 0.781 0.819" style="vertical-align: -0.152em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑄</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;queries, it moves&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><span style="display: inline;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.732em" height="0.68em" viewBox="0 -0.669 0.732 0.68" style="vertical-align: -0.011em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑂</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.333em" height="0.853em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.333 0.853" style="vertical-align: -0.177em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">(</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.781em" height="0.819em" viewBox="0 -0.667 0.781 0.819" style="vertical-align: -0.152em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑄</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="1.879em" height="1.331em" viewBox="0 -1.1155 1.879 1.331" style="vertical-align: -0.2155em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.928,0)">𝑁</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.333em" height="0.853em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.333 0.853" style="vertical-align: -0.177em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">)</text></svg></div></span></span></span>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; margin-block: var(--EPacR--Mhy5Ac,0) var(--EPacR--tlBMye,12px); padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">The&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝑅</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.74em" height="0.653em" viewBox="0 -0.653 0.74 0.653" style="vertical-align: 0em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑅</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;pointer:</span>&nbsp;While&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝐿</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.708em" height="0.653em" viewBox="0 -0.653 0.708 0.653" style="vertical-align: 0em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝐿</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;is stuck in one block,&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝑅</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.74em" height="0.653em" viewBox="0 -0.653 0.74 0.653" style="vertical-align: 0em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑅</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;only moves in&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">one direction</span>&nbsp;(from left to right) across the whole array. Once&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝐿</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.708em" height="0.653em" viewBox="0 -0.653 0.708 0.653" style="vertical-align: 0em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝐿</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;finally moves to the&nbsp;<em style="font-weight: inherit;">next</em>&nbsp;block,&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝑅</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.74em" height="0.653em" viewBox="0 -0.653 0.74 0.653" style="vertical-align: 0em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑅</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;resets and starts its march again. Since there are&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><msqrt><mi>𝑁</mi></msqrt></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="1.879em" height="1.331em" viewBox="0 -1.1155 1.879 1.331" style="vertical-align: -0.2155em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.928,0)">𝑁</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,-0.0435)">√</text><line x1="0.928" y1="-0.9835" x2="1.879" y2="-0.9835" stroke-width="0.066" stroke="#E6E8F0"></line></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;blocks and&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝑅</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.74em" height="0.653em" viewBox="0 -0.653 0.74 0.653" style="vertical-align: 0em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑅</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;can move&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝑁</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.851em" height="0.653em" viewBox="0 -0.653 0.851 0.653" style="vertical-align: 0em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑁</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;steps per block, it moves&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><span style="display: inline;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.732em" height="0.68em" viewBox="0 -0.669 0.732 0.68" style="vertical-align: -0.011em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑂</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.333em" height="0.853em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.333 0.853" style="vertical-align: -0.177em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">(</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.851em" height="0.653em" viewBox="0 -0.653 0.851 0.653" style="vertical-align: 0em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑁</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="1.879em" height="1.331em" viewBox="0 -1.1155 1.879 1.331" style="vertical-align: -0.2155em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.928,0)">𝑁</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,-0.0435)">√</text><line x1="0.928" y1="-0.9835" x2="1.879" y2="-0.9835" stroke-width="0.066" stroke="#E6E8F0"></line></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.333em" height="0.853em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.333 0.853" style="vertical-align: -0.177em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">)</text></svg></div></span></span></span>&nbsp;total.</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">3. The "Snake" Optimization (Hilbert Curve / Zig-Zag)<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝐿</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.708em" height="0.653em" viewBox="0 -0.653 0.708 0.653" style="vertical-align: 0em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝐿</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;moves to a new block,&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math transform="translate(0,0)">𝑅</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;might have to jump from the far right all the way back to the left.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">To optimize this, we use a&nbsp;<span font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; Sort&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">This way, when&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: By sorting,&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝑅</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.74em" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑅</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;moves steadily forward within each block, significantly reducing the "distance" it travels.<span><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 73.5078px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, min-width: 0px;">YouTube</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: style="font-weight: 700;">Zig-Zag optimization</span>&nbsp;that prevents&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); If you know the distinct count of&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">[0, 2]</code>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">[3, 5]</code>, you cannot simply add them together to get the count for&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">[0, 5]</code>&nbsp;because the same numbers might appear in both ranges. This makes Prefix Sums or Segment Trees very difficult (or impossible) to use directly.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Scenario: The "Unique ID" Problem<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Query:</span>&nbsp;How many&nbsp;<em style="font-weight: inherit;">unique</em>&nbsp;users visited between index&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">1</code>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Mo's uses a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Frequency Array</span>&nbsp;(or Hash Map) and a&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">distinct_count</code>&nbsp;variable.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ol style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 20px;"><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal; margin-block: 0px 12px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;"><code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">add(index)</code></span>:</span><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: var(--EPacR--tQAWtd,12px) var(--EPacR--fHZGNe,16px); font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; margin-block: var(--EPacR--Mhy5Ac,0) var(--EPacR--tlBMye,12px); padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Look at the ID at that index.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; margin-block: var(--EPacR--Mhy5Ac,0) var(--EPacR--tlBMye,12px); padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Increment its frequency:&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">freq[ID]++</code>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; margin-block: var(--EPacR--Mhy5Ac,0) var(--EPacR--tlBMye,12px); padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">If the frequency just became&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">1</span>, it’s a new unique element:&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">distinct_count++</code>.</span></li></ul></li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal; margin-block: 0px 12px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;"><code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">remove(index)</code></span>:</span><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: var(--EPacR--tQAWtd,12px) var(--EPacR--fHZGNe,16px); font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; margin-block: var(--EPacR--Mhy5Ac,0) var(--EPacR--tlBMye,12px); padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Look at the ID at that index.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; margin-block: var(--EPacR--Mhy5Ac,0) var(--EPacR--tlBMye,12px); padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Decrement its frequency:&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">freq[ID]--</code>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; margin-block: var(--EPacR--Mhy5Ac,0) var(--EPacR--tlBMye,12px); padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">If the frequency just became&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">0</span>, we lost a unique element:&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">l</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.278,0)">o</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.778,0)">g</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(1.4447,0)">𝑁</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.333em" height="0.853em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.333 0.853" style="vertical-align: -0.177em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">)</text></svg></div></span></span></span></span>. For&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><span style="display: inline;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.851em" height="0.653em" viewBox="0 -0.653 0.851 0.653" style="vertical-align: 0em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑁</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="2.6566em" height="0.93em" viewBox="0 -0.916 2.6566 0.93" style="vertical-align: -0.014em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.2778,0)">=</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(1.2406,0)">1</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(1.7406,0)">0</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 0.75px" transform="translate(2.2406,-0.4)">5</text></svg></div></span></span></span>,&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><span style="display: inline;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="2.2957em" height="0.901em" viewBox="0 -0.683 2.2957 0.901" style="vertical-align: -0.218em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">l</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.278,0)">o</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.778,0)">g</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(1.4447,0)">𝑁</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="2.2406em" height="0.684em" viewBox="0 -0.676 2.2406 0.684" style="vertical-align: -0.008em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.2778,0)">≈</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(1.2406,0)">1</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(1.7406,0)">7</text></svg></div></span></span></span>.&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><span style="display: inline;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="1em" height="0.684em" viewBox="0 -0.676 1 0.684" style="vertical-align: -0.008em; overflow: visible; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="2.9886em" height="0.71em" viewBox="0 -0.684 2.9886 0.71" style="vertical-align: -0.026em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.2778,0)">≪</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(1.4886,0)">3</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">2. The "Update" Problem<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Mo’s is designed for&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">static arrays</span>.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: var(--EPacR--tQAWtd,12px) var(--EPacR--fHZGNe,16px); font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; margin-block: var(--EPacR--Mhy5Ac,0) var(--EPacR--tlBMye,12px); padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">If the array values change between queries, standard Mo's fails.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; margin-block: var(--EPacR--Mhy5Ac,0) var(--EPacR--tlBMye,12px); padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">You&nbsp;<em style="font-weight: inherit;">can</em>&nbsp;use&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">3D Mo's Algorithm</span>&nbsp;(which adds a "time" dimension), but the complexity jumps to&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;"><span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><span style="display: inline;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.732em" height="0.68em" viewBox="0 -0.669 0.732 0.68" style="vertical-align: -0.011em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑂</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.333em" height="0.853em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.333 0.853" style="vertical-align: -0.177em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">(</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="1.9405em" height="0.916em" viewBox="0 -0.916 1.9405 0.916" style="vertical-align: 0em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑁</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 0.75px" transform="translate(0.941,-0.4)">5</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 0.75px" transform="translate(1.316,-0.4)">/</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 0.75px" transform="translate(1.5245,-0.4)">3</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.333em" height="0.853em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.333 0.853" style="vertical-align: -0.177em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">)</text></svg></div></span></span></span></span>. This is much slower than a Segment Tree, which handles updates and queries both in&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><span style="display: inline;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.732em" height="0.68em" viewBox="0 -0.669 0.732 0.68" style="vertical-align: -0.011em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑂</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.333em" height="0.853em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.333 0.853" style="vertical-align: -0.177em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">(</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="2.2957em" height="0.901em" viewBox="0 -0.683 2.2957 0.901" style="vertical-align: -0.218em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">l</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.278,0)">o</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.778,0)">g</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(1.4447,0)">𝑁</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.333em" height="0.853em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.333 0.853" style="vertical-align: -0.177em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">)</text></svg></div></span></span></span>.</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">3. High Constant Factor<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Even if the big-O complexity looks okay, Mo's moves pointers millions of times.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: var(--EPacR--tQAWtd,12px) var(--EPacR--fHZGNe,16px); font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; margin-block: var(--EPacR--Mhy5Ac,0) var(--EPacR--tlBMye,12px); padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">If your&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">add()</code>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">remove()</code>&nbsp;functions are slow (e.g., they use a&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">std::map</code>&nbsp;or complex logic), the constant factor will kill the performance.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; margin-block: var(--EPacR--Mhy5Ac,0) var(--EPacR--tlBMye,12px); padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Example:</span>&nbsp;For "Range Sum," Mo's is overkill. A Prefix Sum array is&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><span style="display: inline;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.732em" height="0.68em" viewBox="0 -0.669 0.732 0.68" style="vertical-align: -0.011em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑂</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.333em" height="0.853em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.333 0.853" style="vertical-align: -0.177em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">(</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.5em" height="0.676em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.5 0.676" style="vertical-align: 0em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">1</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.333em" height="0.853em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.333 0.853" style="vertical-align: -0.177em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">)</text></svg></div></span></span></span>&nbsp;per query. Mo's would be hundreds of times slower.</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">4. Memory Locality (The "Cache" Issue)<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Because Mo's reorders queries, it jumps around the array in a way that isn't always "cache-friendly." While sorting helps, it still involves more memory jumping than a simple linear scan or a compact Segment Tree.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe);
